253→\treturn e.desc\n   254→}\n   255→\n   256→func Error(err error) error {\n   257→\tif err == nil {\n   258→\t\treturn nil\n   259→\t}\n   260→\tverr, ok := errStringToError[ErrorDesc(err)]\n   261→\tif !ok { // not gRPC error\n   262→\t\treturn err\n   263→\t}\n   264→\tev, ok := status.FromError(verr)\n   265→\tvar desc string\n   266→\tif ok {\n   267→\t\tdesc = ev.Message()\n   268→\t} else {\n   269→\t\tdesc = verr.Error()\n   270→\t}\n   271→\treturn EtcdError{code: ev.Code(), desc: desc}\n   272→}\n   273→\n   274→func ErrorDesc(err error) string {\n   275→\tif s, ok := status.FromError(err); ok {\n   276→\t\treturn s.Message()\n   277→\t}\n   278→\treturn err.Error()\n   279→}\n   280→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it
